Wright">Wright, Rita P.</a> (2010). <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=gAgFPQAACAAJ" rel="nofollow"><i>The Ancient Indus: Urbanism, Economy, and Society</i></a>. <a href="/wiki/Cambridge_University_Press_%26_Assessment" title="Cambridge University Press &amp; Assessment">Cambridge University Press</a>. pp. 115–125. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISBN_(identifier)" title="ISBN (identifier)">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-521-57219-4" title="Special:BookSources/978-0-521-57219-4"><bdi>978-0-521-57219-4</bdi></a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=The+Ancient+Indus%3A+Urbanism%2C+Economy%2C+and+Society&amp;rft.pages=115-125&amp;rft.pub=Cambridge+University+Press&amp;rft.date=2010&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-521-57219-4&amp;rft.aulast=Wright&amp;rft.aufirst=Rita+P.&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3DgAgFPQAACAAJ&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ABronze+Age"></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-63"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-63">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation book cs1" id="CITEREFDyson2018"><a href="/wiki/Tim_Dyson" title="Tim Dyson">Dyson, Tim</a> (2018). <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=3TRtDwAAQBAJ&amp;pg=PA29" rel="nofollow"><i>A Population History of India: From the First Modern People to the Present Day</i></a>. <a href="/wiki/Oxford_University_Press" title="Oxford University Press">Oxford University Press</a>. p. 29. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISBN_(identifier)" title="ISBN (identifier)">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-19-882905-8" title="Special:BookSources/978-0-19-882905-8"><bdi>978-0-19-882905-8</bdi></a>. <q>Mohenjo-daro and Harappa may each have contained between 30,000 and 60,000 people (perhaps more in the former case). Water transport was crucial for the provisioning of these and other cities. That said, the vast majority of people lived in rural areas. At the height of the Indus valley civilization the subcontinent may have contained 4-6 million people.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=A+Population+History+of+India%3A+From+the+First+Modern+People+to+the+Present+Day&amp;rft.pages=29&amp;rft.pub=Oxford+University+Press&amp;rft.date=2018&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-19-882905-8&amp;rft.aulast=Dyson&amp;rft.aufirst=Tim&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3D3TRtDwAAQBAJ%26pg%3DPA29&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ABronze+Age"></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-64"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-64">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation book cs1" id="CITEREFMcIntosh2008"><a href="/wiki/Jane_McIntosh" title="Jane McIntosh">McIntosh, Jane</a> (2008). <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=1AJO2A-CbccC" rel="nofollow"><i>The Ancient Indus Valley: New Perspectives</i></a>. <a href="/wiki/ABC-Clio" title="ABC-Clio">ABC-Clio</a>. p. 387. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISBN_(identifier)" title="ISBN (identifier)">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-1-57607-907-2" title="Special:BookSources/978-1-57607-907-2"><bdi>978-1-57607-907-2</bdi></a>. <q>The enormous potential of the greater Indus region offered scope for huge population increase; by the end of the Mature Harappan period, the Harappans are estimated to have numbered somewhere between 1 and 5 million, probably well below the region's carrying capacity.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=The+Ancient+Indus+Valley%3A+New+Perspectives&amp;rft.pages=387&amp;rft.pub=ABC-Clio&amp;rft.date=2008&amp;rft.isbn=978-1-57607-907-2&amp;rft.aulast=McIntosh&amp;rft.aufirst=Jane&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3D1AJO2A-CbccC&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ABronze+Age"></span></span>
